\DoxyCodeLine{04408\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ lastIsNan\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{04409\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04410\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ lastIsNan\ =\ \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{04411\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ++i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04412\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04413\ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04414\ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{04415\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ segmentStart\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04416\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ i\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04417\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ lineDataSize\ =\ lineData.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{04418\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}\ (i\ <\ lineDataSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{04419\ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{04420\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (qIsNaN(lineData.at(i).y())\ ||\ qIsNaN(lineData.at(i).x())\ ||\ qIsInf(lineData.at(i).y()))\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NaNs\ create\ a\ gap\ in\ the\ line.\ Also\ filter\ Infs\ which\ make\ drawPolyline\ block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04421\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{04422\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ painter-\/>drawPolyline(lineData.constData()+segmentStart,\ i-\/segmentStart);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ i,\ because\ we\ don't\ want\ to\ include\ the\ current\ NaN\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04423\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ segmentStart\ =\ i+1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04424\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04425\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ++i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04426\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04427\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ draw\ last\ segment:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04428\ \ \ \ \ painter-\/>drawPolyline(lineData.constData()+segmentStart,\ lineDataSize-\/segmentStart);}
\DoxyCodeLine{04429\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04430\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04431\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ end\ of\ 'src/plottable1d.cpp'\ */}}
